   680→        /**
   681→         * Replaces image references in markdown with base64 data URLs from encrypted content

   683→        async replaceImagesWithBase64(markdownContent) {
   684→            let processedContent = markdownContent;
   685→            
   686→            // Find all image references in markdown: ![alt](path)
   687→            const imagePattern = /!\[([^\]]*)\]\(([^)]+)\)/g;
   688→            const matches = [...markdownContent.matchAll(imagePattern)];

   702→                    const dataUrl = `data:${mimeType};base64,${base64Content}`;
   703→                    
   704→                    // Replace the image reference with base64 data URL
   705→                    processedContent = processedContent.replace(fullMatch, `![${altText}](${dataUrl})`);
   706→                    console.log(`✅ Replaced image ${normalizedPath} with base64 data URL`);
   707→                } else {
   708→                    // If not in encrypted content, it might be a shared image
   709→                    // Keep the original path but adjust for correct web path
   710→                    if (imagePath.includes('../../00_intro/images/')) {
   711→                        // Shared images - adjust path for web access
   712→                        const webPath = imagePath.replace('../../', '/agentic-ai-nano/');
   713→                        processedContent = processedContent.replace(fullMatch, `![${altText}](${webPath})`);
   714→                        console.log(`📷 Using shared image with web path: ${webPath}`);
   715→                    } else {
   716→                        console.warn(`❌ Image not found in encrypted content: ${normalizedPath}`);
   717→                        console.log('Available encrypted images:', Object.keys(this.loadedContent).filter(key => key.match(/\.(png|jpg|jpeg|gif|svg)$/i)));
   718→                    }
   719→                }
   720→            }
   721→            
   722→            return processedContent;
   723→        }

     1→#!/usr/bin/env node
     2→
     3→/**
     4→ * Post-build script to inject encrypted corporate content into HTML files
     5→ * This ensures the corporate content loader can find the encrypted data
     6→ */
     7→
     8→const fs = require('fs');
     9→const path = require('path');
    10→
    11→const SITE_DIR = path.join(__dirname, '..', 'site');
    12→const ENCRYPTED_CONTENT_PATH = path.join(__dirname, '..', 'docs-content', 'corporate-only', 'content.encrypted.json');
    13→
    14→console.log('🔐 Injecting encrypted corporate content into HTML files...');
    15→
    16→// Read encrypted content
    17→let encryptedContent;
    18→try {
    19→    encryptedContent = fs.readFileSync(ENCRYPTED_CONTENT_PATH, 'utf8');
    20→    console.log('✅ Loaded encrypted content from:', ENCRYPTED_CONTENT_PATH);
    21→} catch (error) {
    22→    console.error('❌ Failed to load encrypted content:', error.message);
    23→    process.exit(1);
    24→}
    25→
    26→// Function to inject content into HTML file
    27→function injectContentIntoHtml(filePath) {
    28→    try {
    29→        let htmlContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
    30→        
    31→        // Check if already injected to avoid duplicates
    32→        if (htmlContent.includes('ENCRYPTED_CORPORATE_CONTENT_START')) {
    33→            console.log('⏭️  Already injected:', path.relative(SITE_DIR, filePath));
    34→            return;
    35→        }
    36→        
    37→        // Create injection comment
    38→        const injectionComment = `
    39→<!-- ENCRYPTED_CORPORATE_CONTENT_START
    40→${encryptedContent}
    41→ENCRYPTED_CORPORATE_CONTENT_END -->`;
    42→        
    43→        // Inject before closing body tag
    44→        if (htmlContent.includes('</body>')) {
    45→            htmlContent = htmlContent.replace('</body>', `${injectionComment}\n</body>`);
    46→            fs.writeFileSync(filePath, htmlContent, 'utf8');
    47→            console.log('✅ Injected into:', path.relative(SITE_DIR, filePath));
    48→        } else {
    49→            console.log('⚠️  No </body> tag found in:', path.relative(SITE_DIR, filePath));
    50→        }
    51→    } catch (error) {
    52→        console.error('❌ Failed to inject into', filePath, ':', error.message);
    53→    }
    54→}
    55→
    56→// Recursively find and process HTML files
    57→function processDirectory(dirPath) {
    58→    const entries = fs.readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
    59→    
    60→    for (const entry of entries) {
    61→        const fullPath = path.join(dirPath, entry.name);
    62→        
    63→        if (entry.isDirectory()) {
    64→            processDirectory(fullPath);
    65→        } else if (entry.isFile() && entry.name.endsWith('.html')) {
    66→            injectContentIntoHtml(fullPath);
    67→        }
    68→    }
    69→}
    70→
    71→// Start processing
    72→if (!fs.existsSync(SITE_DIR)) {
    73→    console.error('❌ Site directory not found:', SITE_DIR);
    74→    console.log('💡 Run "mkdocs build" first to generate the site');
    75→    process.exit(1);
    76→}
    77→
    78→console.log('🔍 Processing HTML files in:', SITE_DIR);
    79→processDirectory(SITE_DIR);
    80→
    81→console.log('🎉 Corporate content injection complete!');

     5→### **Module Overview**
     6→
     7→In an era where software systems must be intelligent, adaptive, and capable of autonomous decision-making, traditional programming approaches are reaching their limits. Data pipelines now need to handle ambiguous requirements, APIs must reason about context, and systems must adapt to changing conditions without constant human intervention. This self-paced 2-week module provides comprehensive instruction on building production-ready AI agents using 2025 state-of-the-art frameworks and implementing the five core agentic patterns: Reflection, Tool Use, ReAct, Planning, and Multi-Agent Collaboration. Through hands-on tutorials and progressive implementation, you'll master cutting-edge agent development with performance breakthroughs (CrewAI 5.76x faster execution), distributed system production capabilities, and modern protocol standardization (MCP, A2A, ACP, ANP). You'll develop skills to create intelligent, adaptable agents using both bare-metal approaches and established frameworks optimized for 2025 production environments.

    26→    // Check if current page is configured for corporate content
    27→    function isPageConfiguredForCorporateContent() {
    28→        const currentPath = window.location.pathname;
    29→        const currentHash = window.location.hash;
    30→        
    31→        for (const [path, config] of Object.entries(CORPORATE_CONTENT_PAGES)) {
    32→            if (!config.enabled) continue;
    33→            
    34→            // Check if current path matches
    35→            if (currentPath.includes(path)) {
    36→                return true;
    37→            }
    38→            
    39→            // Check if hash triggers match
    40→            if (config.hashTriggers && config.hashTriggers.length > 0) {
    41→                for (const trigger of config.hashTriggers) {
    42→                    if (currentHash.includes(trigger)) {
    43→                        return true;
    44→                    }
    45→                }
    46→            }
    47→        }
    48→        
    49→        return false;
    50→    }

    67→    // BMW corporate network detection
    68→    function isCorporateNetwork() {
    69→        // Check if accessing from BMW corporate network indicators
    70→        const hostname = window.location.hostname;
    71→        const host = window.location.host;
    72→        
    73→        // Corporate network indicators
    74→        const corporateIndicators = [
    75→            // Internal IP ranges (adjust as needed)
    76→            /^10\./,
    77→            /^192\.168\./,
    78→            /^172\.(1[6-9]|2[0-9]|3[01])\./,
    79→            // BMW-specific domains
    80→            /bmw\.com$/,
    81→            /bmwgroup\.com$/
    82→        ];
    83→
    84→        // Check hostname against corporate patterns
    85→        for (const pattern of corporateIndicators) {
    86→            if (pattern.test(hostname) || pattern.test(host)) {
    87→                console.log('Corporate network detected via hostname:', hostname);
    88→                return true;
    89→            }
    90→        }
    91→
    92→        // For development/testing - check if we're on GitHub Pages from public internet
    93→        if (hostname.includes('github.io')) {
    94→            console.log('GitHub Pages detected - showing public content');
    95→            return false;
    96→        }
    97→
    98→        // For localhost/127.0.0.1 - let the CN detection determine access
    99→        if (hostname === 'localhost' || hostname === '127.0.0.1') {
   100→            console.log('Localhost detected - running CN detection to determine access');
   101→            return false; // Let checkInternalService() determine corporate access
   102→        }
   103→
   104→        // Check user agent or other indicators that might suggest corporate network
   105→        // This is a fallback check
   106→        console.log('No corporate network indicators found for hostname:', hostname);
   107→
   108→        // Default to public network if no corporate indicators found
   109→        return false;
   110→    }

   112→    function checkInternalService() {
   113→        // Run internal service check to detect corporate network access
   114→        console.log('Running internal service check to detect corporate network access');
   115→        
   116→        // Show initial status
   117→        updateNetworkStatusIndicator('checking');

   119→        // Try multiple detection methods
   120→        let detectionComplete = false;
   121→        
   122→        // Method 1: URL parameter override REMOVED to prevent manual corporate mode switching
   123→        
   124→        // Method 2: Check external IP first, then try internal service
   125→        console.log('🔍 Checking BMW network access');
   126→        console.log('🌍 Current hostname:', window.location.hostname);
   127→        console.log('🌍 Current URL:', window.location.href);
   128→        
   129→        // Check external IP for BMW ranges (this was working before!)
   130→        fetch('https://api.ipify.org?format=json')
   131→            .then(response => response.json())
   132→            .then(data => {
   133→                console.log('🌐 External IP detected:', data.ip);
   134→                // BMW corporate IP ranges
   135→                const corporateIPPatterns = [
   136→                    /^160\.46\./,    // Your working IP range
   137→                    /^194\.114\./,   // BMW public IP range
   138→                    /^195\.34\./,    // BMW public IP range
   139→                    /^212\.204\./    // BMW public IP range
   140→                ];
   141→                
   142→                const isCorporateIP = corporateIPPatterns.some(pattern => {
   143→                    if (pattern.test(data.ip)) {
   144→                        console.log(`✅ IP ${data.ip} matches corporate pattern: ${pattern}`);
   145→                        return true;
   146→                    }
   147→                    return false;
   148→                });
   149→                
   150→                if (isCorporateIP && !detectionComplete) {
   151→                    console.log('✅ Corporate IP range detected - showing corporate content');
   152→                    detectionComplete = true;
   153→                    showCorporateContent();
   154→                } else if (!detectionComplete) {
   155→                    console.log(`📍 IP ${data.ip} not in corporate ranges, trying internal service check`);
   156→                    tryInternalServiceCheck();
   157→                }
   158→            })
   159→            .catch(error => {
   160→                console.log('❌ IP detection failed, trying internal service check:', error);
   161→                tryInternalServiceCheck();
   162→            });
   163→            
   164→        function tryInternalServiceCheck() {
   165→            if (detectionComplete) return;
   166→            
   167→            // Try internal service check with BMW Content Hub only (no 10.x latency)
   168→            const testUrls = [
   169→                'https://contenthub.bmwgroup.net/favicon.ico'  // BMW Content Hub (most reliable, no VPN latency)
   170→            ];
   171→            
   172→            let urlIndex = 0;
   173→            
   174→            function testNextUrl() {
   175→                if (urlIndex >= testUrls.length || detectionComplete) {
   176→                    // All URLs failed
   177→                    if (!detectionComplete) {
   178→                        console.log('❌ All internal service checks failed - showing public content');
   179→                        hideCorporateContent();
   180→                        detectionComplete = true;
   181→                    }
   182→                    return;
   183→                }
   184→                
   185→                const testUrl = testUrls[urlIndex];
   186→                console.log(`🔍 Trying internal service: ${testUrl}`);
   187→                
   188→                const img = new Image();
   189→                img.onload = function() {
   190→                    if (!detectionComplete) {
   191→                        console.log('✅ Internal service reachable - showing corporate content');
   192→                        showCorporateContent();
   193→                        detectionComplete = true;
   194→                    }
   195→                };
   196→                img.onerror = function() {
   197→                    console.log(`❌ Failed to reach: ${testUrl}`);
   198→                    urlIndex++;
   199→                    setTimeout(testNextUrl, 500); // Try next URL after short delay
   200→                };
   201→                
   202→                img.src = testUrl + '?' + Date.now();
   203→            }
   204→            
   205→            testNextUrl();
   206→        }
   207→        
   208→        // Set a timeout to ensure we don't wait forever  
   209→        setTimeout(() => {
   210→            if (!detectionComplete) {
   211→                console.log('⏱️ BMW ContentHub check timed out after 2s - defaulting to public content');
   212→                hideCorporateContent();
   213→                detectionComplete = true;
   214→            }
   215→        }, 2000);
   216→    }

   471→    function cleanupNavigationState() {
   472→        // Clean up any previous navigation state
   473→        // We're on a corporate page, so just reset for fresh setup
   474→        if (window.corporateScrollListener) {
   475→            window.removeEventListener('scroll', window.corporateScrollListener);
   476→            window.corporateScrollListener = null;
   477→            console.log('🧹 Cleaned up previous corporate scroll listener');
   478→        }

   480→
   481→    // Initialize when DOM is ready and on every page load
   482→    function runDetection() {
   483→        // Prevent multiple simultaneous detections
   484→        if (detectionInProgress) {
   485→            console.log('🔄 Detection already in progress, skipping...');
   486→            return;
   487→        }
   488→        
   489→        // Clear any pending detection
   490→        if (detectionTimeout) {
   491→            clearTimeout(detectionTimeout);
   492→        }
   493→        
   494→        // Aggressive debounce to prevent rapid successive calls from different event sources
   495→        detectionTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
   496→            // Double-check as detection might have been triggered by another source
   497→            if (detectionInProgress) {
   498→                console.log('🔄 Detection started by another trigger, skipping...');
   499→                return;
   500→            }
   501→            
   502→            detectionInProgress = true;
   503→            console.log('🔄 Starting fresh network detection...');
   504→            
   505→            // Clean up navigation state first
   506→            cleanupNavigationState();
   507→            
   508→            try {
   509→                initializeNetworkDetection();
   510→            } finally {
   511→                // Reset detection flag after longer delay to prevent rapid re-runs
   512→                setTimeout(() => {
   513→                    detectionInProgress = false;
   514→                    console.log('✅ Network detection cycle complete, ready for next run');
   515→                }, 5000); // Increased from 2000 to 5000ms
   516→            }
   517→        }, 300); // Increased from 100 to 300ms debounce delay
   518→    }
   519→    
   520→    // Initial run
   521→    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
   522→        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', runDetection);
   523→    } else {
   524→        runDetection();
   525→    }
   526→    
   527→    // Set up navigation listeners immediately (not waiting for DOMContentLoaded)
   528→    console.log('🎯 Setting up navigation listeners');
   529→    
   530→    // Watch for URL changes with MutationObserver
   531→    let lastUrl = location.href;
   532→    const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
   533→        const url = location.href;
   534→        if (url !== lastUrl) {
   535→            lastUrl = url;
   536→            console.log('📍 URL changed to:', url);
   537→            
   538→            // Reset Session 10 loaded flag when navigating to different pages
   539→            if (!url.includes('session10-corporate') && !url.includes('Session10_Enterprise_Integration')) {
   540→                session10Loaded = false;
   541→            }
   542→            
   543→            // No cleanup needed - if we navigate away, the page will reload
   544→            // and our early exit will prevent this code from running
   545→            
   546→            setTimeout(runDetection, 100);
   547→        }
   548→    });
   549→    observer.observe(document.body || document.documentElement, {
   550→        subtree: true, 
   551→        childList: true
   552→    });
   553→    
   554→    // Listen for navigation link clicks (use capturing to catch all clicks)
   555→    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   556→        const link = e.target.closest('a');
   557→        if (link) {
   558→            const href = link.getAttribute('href');
   559→            console.log('🔗 Link clicked:', href);
   560→            if (link.classList.contains('md-nav__link') || 
   561→                link.classList.contains('md-tabs__link') ||
   562→                href?.includes('/00_intro/')) {
   563→                console.log('🔗 Navigation link detected, will re-run detection');
   564→                setTimeout(runDetection, 500);
   565→            }
   566→        }
   567→    }, true); // Use capture phase
   568→    
   569→    // Also listen for popstate
   570→    window.addEventListener('popstate', () => {
   571→        console.log('⬅️ Browser navigation detected');
   572→        
   573→        // Reset Session 10 loaded flag when navigating back/forward
   574→        const url = location.href;
   575→        if (!url.includes('session10-corporate') && !url.includes('Session10_Enterprise_Integration')) {
   576→            session10Loaded = false;
   577→        }
   578→        
   579→        runDetection();
   580→    });

   591→                linkText.includes('Testing Your Connection') ||
   592→                linkText.includes('Available Models') ||
   593→                linkText.includes('Using in Code') ||
   594→                linkText.includes('Framework Integration') ||
   595→                linkText.includes('Why Cloud Development?') ||
   596→                linkText.includes('AI Assistant Integration')) {
   597→                const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   598→                if (listItem) {
   599→                    console.log('Hiding corporate nav item:', linkText);
   600→                    listItem.style.display = 'none';
   601→                }
   602→            }
   603→        });
   604→    }
   605→
   606→    function showCorporateNavigationItems() {
   607→        const navigationItems = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
   608→        navigationItems.forEach(link => {
   609→            const linkText = link.textContent.trim();
   610→            // Show items that contain corporate/BMW content indicators
   611→            if (linkText.includes('BMW Gaia LLM API') || 
   612→                linkText.includes('BMW Cloud Development Environment with Coder') ||
   613→                linkText.includes('Quick Setup') ||
   614→                linkText.includes('Testing Your Connection') ||
   615→                linkText.includes('Available Models') ||
   616→                linkText.includes('Using in Code') ||
   617→                linkText.includes('Framework Integration') ||
   618→                linkText.includes('Why Cloud Development?') ||
   619→                linkText.includes('AI Assistant Integration')) {
   620→                const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   621→                if (listItem) {
   622→                    console.log('Showing corporate nav item:', linkText);
   623→                    listItem.style.display = '';
   624→                }
   625→            }
   626→        });
   627→        
   628→        // Add Session 10 to Module 03 navigation when in corporate mode
   629→        addSession10Navigation();
   630→    }
   631→
   632→    function addSession10Navigation() {
   633→        // Find Session 9 in Module 03 navigation and add Session 10 after it
   634→        const session9Link = document.querySelector('a[href*="Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment"]');
   635→        if (session9Link) {
   636→            const session9Item = session9Link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   637→            
   638→            // Check for ANY existing Session 10 navigation items - not just corporate ones
   639→            const existingSession10 = document.querySelector('a[href*="session10"], a[href*="Session10"], .bmw-corporate-nav-item, a[href*="Enterprise_Integration"]');
   640→            
   641→            if (session9Item && !existingSession10) {
   642→                console.log('🔧 Adding Session 10 to corporate navigation');
   643→                
   644→                // Create Session 10 navigation item
   645→                const session10Item = document.createElement('li');
   646→                session10Item.className = 'md-nav__item bmw-corporate-nav-item';
   647→                
   648→                const session10Link = document.createElement('a');
   649→                session10Link.href = '#session10-corporate-only';
   650→                session10Link.className = 'md-nav__link bmw-corporate-link';
   651→                session10Link.textContent = 'Session 10 - Enterprise Integration';
   652→                
   653→                // Add click handler to load corporate content
   654→                session10Link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   655→                    e.preventDefault();
   656→                    loadCorporateSession10();
   657→                });
   658→                
   659→                session10Item.appendChild(session10Link);
   660→                
   661→                // Insert after Session 9
   662→                session9Item.parentNode.insertBefore(session10Item, session9Item.nextSibling);
   663→                
   664→                console.log('✅ Session 10 added to corporate navigation');
   665→            } else if (existingSession10) {
   666→                console.log('📄 Session 10 navigation already exists, skipping creation');
   667→            }
   668→        }
   669→        
   670→        // Also update the "Next" link on Session 9 to point to Session 10
   671→        updateSession9NextLink();
   672→    }

   675→        // Find "Next" navigation links and update Session 9 to point to Session 10
   676→        const nextLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.md-footer__link--next');
   677→        nextLinks.forEach(link => {
   678→            if (window.location.pathname.includes('Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment')) {

   682→                    link.href = '#session10-corporate-only';
   683→

   685→                    link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   686→                        e.preventDefault();
   687→                        loadCorporateSession10();
   688→                    });
   689→                    
   690→                    console.log('🔧 Updated Session 9 next link to point to Session 10');
   691→                }
   692→            }
   693→        });
   694→    }
   695→
   696→    // Track if Session 10 content is currently loaded to prevent multiple loads
   697→    let session10Loaded = false;
   698→    
   699→    window.loadCorporateSession10 = async function() {
   700→        console.log('🔐 Loading corporate Session 10 content...');
   701→        
   702→        // Prevent multiple loads of Session 10 content
   703→        if (session10Loaded) {
   704→            console.log('📄 Session 10 already loaded, skipping...');
   705→            return true;
   706→        }
   707→        
   708→        // Retry mechanism for improved reliability
   709→        const maxRetries = 3;
   710→        let retryCount = 0;
   711→        
   712→        while (retryCount < maxRetries) {
   713→            try {
   714→                console.log(`🔄 Attempt ${retryCount + 1}/${maxRetries} to load Session 10...`);
   715→                
   716→                // Check if corporate content loader exists
   717→                if (!window.CorporateContentLoader) {
   718→                    console.warn('⚠️ Corporate content loader not available, waiting...');
   719→                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
   720→                    retryCount++;
   721→                    continue;
   722→                }
   723→                
   724→                // If content is not loaded yet, try to load it first
   725→                if (!window.CorporateContentLoader.loadedContent) {
   726→                    console.log('📥 Corporate content not loaded yet, loading now...');
   727→                    const loaded = await window.CorporateContentLoader.load();
   728→                    if (!loaded) {
   729→                        console.warn('⚠️ Failed to load corporate content, retrying...');
   730→                        retryCount++;
   731→                        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
   732→                        continue;
   733→                    }
   734→                    console.log('✅ Corporate content loaded successfully');
   735→                }
   736→                
   737→                // Now check for Session 10 content
   738→                const session10Content = window.CorporateContentLoader.loadedContent['03_mcp-acp-a2a/Session10_Enterprise_Integration_Production_Deployment.md'];
   739→                if (session10Content) {
   740→                    console.log('📄 Found Session 10 content, replacing page...');
   741→                    session10Loaded = true;
   742→                    
   743→                    // Update page title
   744→                    document.title = 'Session 10: Enterprise Integration & Production Deployment | Agentic AI Nano-Degree';
   745→                    
   746→                    // Update URL without causing page reload - use hash instead of path to avoid 404s
   747→                    if (history.pushState) {
   748→                        // Use hash-based navigation to avoid creating non-existent paths
   749→                        const baseUrl = window.location.pathname.replace(/#.*$/, '');
   750→                        const newUrl = baseUrl + '#session10-corporate-content';
   751→                        history.pushState({page: 'session10'}, '', newUrl);
   752→                    }
   753→                    
   754→                    // Replace page content
   755→                    await window.CorporateContentLoader.replacePageContent(session10Content);
   756→                    
   757→                    // Wait a bit for content to be injected, then update navigation
   758→                    setTimeout(async () => {
   759→                        await updateMkDocsNavigationForCorporateContent(session10Content);
   760→                    }, 100);
   761→                    
   762→                    // Instantly jump to top of the page after content is loaded
   763→                    setTimeout(() => {
   764→                        window.scrollTo(0, 0);
   765→                        console.log('📍 Jumped to top of Session 10 content');
   766→                    }, 200);
   767→                    
   768→                    console.log('✅ Session 10 corporate content loaded successfully');
   769→                    return true;
   770→                    
   771→                } else {
   772→                    console.warn('⚠️ Session 10 content not found in encrypted data, retrying...');
   773→                    console.log('Available content keys:', Object.keys(window.CorporateContentLoader.loadedContent || {}));
   774→                    retryCount++;
   775→                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
   776→                    continue;
   777→                }
   778→                
   779→            } catch (error) {
   780→                console.warn(`⚠️ Error loading Session 10 (attempt ${retryCount + 1}):`, error);
   781→                retryCount++;
   782→                if (retryCount < maxRetries) {
   783→                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
   784→                }
   785→            }
   786→        }
   787→        
   788→        console.error('❌ Failed to load Session 10 after all retries');
   789→        return false;
   790→    }
   791→
   792→    async function updateMkDocsNavigationForCorporateContent(contentMarkdown) {
   793→        console.log('🔧 Updating MkDocs navigation for corporate content...');
   794→        
   795→        // No guard needed - we're already on a corporate content page if this runs
   796→        
   797→        try {
   798→            // Extract metadata from the content itself
   799→            const contentMetadata = extractContentMetadata(contentMarkdown);
   800→            console.log('📄 Detected content metadata:', contentMetadata);
   801→            
   802→            // Wait for MkDocs navigation to be ready (retry mechanism)
   803→            let attempts = 0;
   804→            const maxAttempts = 5;
   805→            let corporateNavItem = null;
   806→            
   807→            while (!corporateNavItem && attempts < maxAttempts) {
   808→                if (attempts > 0) {
   809→                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 200 * attempts)); // Progressive delay
   810→                }
   811→                
   812→                // Debug: List all navigation links on first attempt
   813→                if (attempts === 0) {
   814→                    const allNavLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
   815→                    console.log('🔍 Debug - All navigation links found:', allNavLinks.length);
   816→                    console.log('🔍 Navigation structure:', Array.from(allNavLinks).slice(0, 10).map(link => ({
   817→                        href: link.getAttribute('href'),
   818→                        text: link.textContent.trim(),
   819→                        active: link.classList.contains('md-nav__link--active')
   820→                    })));
   821→                }
   822→                
   823→                // First try to find current active navigation item
   824→                corporateNavItem = document.querySelector('.md-nav__link--active')?.closest('.md-nav__item');
   825→                
   826→                if (!corporateNavItem) {
   827→                    // Try specific Session 9 patterns
   828→                    const session9Selectors = [
   829→                        'a[href*="Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment"]',
   830→                        'a[href*="Session9"]',
   831→                        'a[href*="Production_Agent_Deployment"]'
   832→                    ];
   833→                    
   834→                    for (const selector of session9Selectors) {
   835→                        corporateNavItem = document.querySelector(selector)?.closest('.md-nav__item');
   836→                        if (corporateNavItem) {
   837→                            console.log(`🎯 Found via selector: ${selector}`);
   838→                            break;
   839→                        }
   840→                    }
   841→                }
   842→                
   843→                if (!corporateNavItem) {
   844→                    // Fallback: try any MCP/ACP section navigation item
   845→                    corporateNavItem = document.querySelector([
   846→                        'a[href*="03_mcp-acp-a2a"]',
   847→                        'a[href*="mcp-acp-a2a"]'
   848→                    ].join(', '))?.closest('.md-nav__item');
   849→                }
   850→                
   851→                attempts++;
   852→                console.log(`🔍 Navigation search attempt ${attempts}/${maxAttempts}, found:`, !!corporateNavItem);
   853→                
   854→                if (corporateNavItem) {
   855→                    const navLink = corporateNavItem.querySelector('.md-nav__link');
   856→                    console.log('🔍 Found navigation item:', {
   857→                        href: navLink?.getAttribute('href'),
   858→                        text: navLink?.textContent?.trim(),
   859→                        outerHTML: corporateNavItem.outerHTML.substring(0, 200) + '...'
   860→                    });
   861→                }
   862→            }
   863→            
   864→            if (corporateNavItem) {
   865→                // Remove active state from all navigation items
   866→                document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__item').forEach(item => {
   867→                    item.classList.remove('md-nav__item--active');
   868→                    const link = item.querySelector('.md-nav__link');
   869→                    if (link) {
   870→                        link.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active');
   871→                    }
   872→                });
   873→                
   874→                // Activate corporate content navigation item
   875→                corporateNavItem.classList.add('md-nav__item--active');
   876→                const corporateLink = corporateNavItem.querySelector('.md-nav__link');
   877→                if (corporateLink) {
   878→                    corporateLink.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
   879→                    // Update the link text to match current content
   880→                    if (contentMetadata.title) {
   881→                        corporateLink.textContent = contentMetadata.title;
   882→                    }
   883→                }
   884→                
   885→                // Create corporate content sub-navigation based on content structure
   886→                createCorporateContentSubNavigation(corporateNavItem, contentMetadata);
   887→                
   888→                // Scroll corporate content item into view in sidebar
   889→                corporateNavItem.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
   890→                
   891→                console.log(`✅ MkDocs navigation updated for ${contentMetadata.title || 'corporate content'}`);
   892→            } else {
   893→                console.warn('⚠️ Corporate content navigation item not found');
   894→            }
   895→            
   896→            // Fix potential sidebar styling conflicts
   897→            fixSidebarStylingConflicts();
   898→            
   899→        } catch (error) {
   900→            console.error('❌ Failed to update MkDocs navigation for corporate content:', error);
   901→        }
   902→    }
   903→
   904→    function extractContentMetadata(markdownContent) {
   905→        const metadata = {
   906→            title: null,
   907→            sections: [],
   908→            type: 'corporate-content'
   909→        };
   910→        
   911→        if (!markdownContent) return metadata;
   912→        
   913→        // Extract title from first H1
   914→        const titleMatch = markdownContent.match(/^#\s+(.+)$/m);
   915→        if (titleMatch) {
   916→            metadata.title = titleMatch[1].trim();
   917→        }
   918→        
   919→        // Extract sections from H2 and H3 headings
   920→        const headingMatches = markdownContent.match(/^#{2,3}\s+(.+)$/gm);
   921→        if (headingMatches) {
   922→            metadata.sections = headingMatches.map(heading => {
   923→                const level = (heading.match(/#/g) || []).length;
   924→                const title = heading.replace(/^#+\s+/, '').trim();
   925→                const id = title.toLowerCase()
   926→                    .replace(/[^a-z0-9\s-]/g, '')
   927→                    .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
   928→                    .replace(/-+/g, '-')
   929→                    .replace(/^-|-$/g, '');
   930→                
   931→                return {
   932→                    level,
   933→                    title,
   934→                    id: id || title.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-'),
   935→                    href: `#${id || title.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-')}`
   936→                };
   937→            });
   938→        }
   939→        
   940→        // Detect content type from title or content
   941→        if (metadata.title) {
   942→            if (metadata.title.includes('Session')) {
   943→                metadata.type = 'session';
   944→                // Extract session number if present
   945→                const sessionMatch = metadata.title.match(/Session\s*(\d+)/i);
   946→                if (sessionMatch) {
   947→                    metadata.sessionNumber = parseInt(sessionMatch[1]);
   948→                }
   949→            } else if (metadata.title.includes('Enterprise') || metadata.title.includes('Production')) {
   950→                metadata.type = 'enterprise-content';
   951→            }
   952→        }
   953→        
   954→        return metadata;
   955→    }
   956→
   957→
   958→    function createCorporateContentSubNavigation(navItem, contentMetadata) {
   959→        console.log(`🔧 Creating sub-navigation for ${contentMetadata.title || 'corporate content'}...`);
   960→        
   961→        // Remove any existing sub-navigation to rebuild with current content
   962→        const existingSubNav = navItem.querySelector('.md-nav');
   963→        if (existingSubNav) {
   964→            existingSubNav.remove();
   965→        }
   966→        
   967→        // Debug content metadata
   968→        console.log('🔍 Content metadata for sub-navigation:', contentMetadata);
   969→        console.log('🔍 Available sections:', contentMetadata.sections);
   970→        
   971→        // Only create sub-navigation if we have sections
   972→        if (contentMetadata.sections && contentMetadata.sections.length > 0) {
   973→            // Create sub-navigation structure
   974→            const subNav = document.createElement('nav');
   975→            subNav.className = 'md-nav md-nav--secondary';
   976→            subNav.setAttribute('aria-label', `${contentMetadata.title || 'Corporate Content'} Navigation`);
   977→            
   978→            const subNavList = document.createElement('ul');
   979→            subNavList.className = 'md-nav__list';
   980→            
   981→            // Create navigation items from content sections
   982→            contentMetadata.sections.forEach(section => {
   983→                const listItem = document.createElement('li');
   984→                listItem.className = 'md-nav__item';
   985→                
   986→                const link = document.createElement('a');
   987→                link.href = section.href;
   988→                link.className = 'md-nav__link';
   989→                link.textContent = section.title;
   990→                
   991→                // Add appropriate nesting class for H3 items
   992→                if (section.level === 3) {
   993→                    listItem.classList.add('md-nav__item--nested');
   994→                }
   995→                
   996→                // Add smooth scroll behavior for anchor links
   997→                link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   998→                    e.preventDefault();
   999→                    const targetId = section.id;
  1000→                    const targetElement = document.getElementById(targetId) || 
  1001→                                         document.querySelector(`h${section.level}[id="${targetId}"]`) ||
  1002→                                         findHeadingByText(section.title);
  1003→                    
  1004→                    if (targetElement) {
  1005→                        targetElement.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
  1006→                        // Update URL hash
  1007→                        history.pushState(null, '', section.href);
  1008→                        
  1009→                        // Update active state in sub-navigation
  1010→                        subNavList.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link').forEach(l => l.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active'));
  1011→                        link.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
  1012→                    }
  1013→                });
  1014→                
  1015→                listItem.appendChild(link);
  1016→                subNavList.appendChild(listItem);
  1017→            });
  1018→            
  1019→            subNav.appendChild(subNavList);
  1020→            navItem.appendChild(subNav);
  1021→            
  1022→            console.log(`✅ Sub-navigation created with ${contentMetadata.sections.length} sections`);
  1023→            
  1024→            // Set up scroll spy for corporate content - we're already on a corporate page
  1025→            setupCorporateContentScrollSpy(subNavList, contentMetadata.sections);
  1026→        }
  1027→        
  1028→        // Mark as corporate content for scroll spy detection
  1029→        document.body.classList.add('corporate-content-active');
  1030→        console.log('🔧 Marked page as corporate content');
  1031→        
  1032→        // Expand the navigation and ensure visibility
  1033→        navItem.classList.add('md-nav__item--nested', 'md-nav__item--active', 'corporate-nav-item');
  1034→        
  1035→        // Make sure the navigation item is visible and expanded
  1036→        const navInput = navItem.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
  1037→        if (navInput) {
  1038→            navInput.checked = true;
  1039→        }
  1040→        
  1041→        // Add explicit CSS to ensure visibility and prevent removal
  1042→        navItem.style.display = 'block !important';
  1043→        navItem.setAttribute('data-corporate-nav', 'true');
  1044→        const subNav = navItem.querySelector('.md-nav');
  1045→        if (subNav) {
  1046→            subNav.style.display = 'block !important';
  1047→            subNav.style.visibility = 'visible';
  1048→            subNav.setAttribute('data-corporate-subnav', 'true');
  1049→        }
  1050→        
  1051→        // Prevent navigation from being hidden by other scripts
  1052→        const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
  1053→            mutations.forEach((mutation) => {
  1054→                if (mutation.type === 'attributes' && mutation.attributeName === 'style') {
  1055→                    const target = mutation.target;
  1056→                    if (target.hasAttribute('data-corporate-nav') || target.hasAttribute('data-corporate-subnav')) {
  1057→                        if (target.style.display === 'none' || target.style.visibility === 'hidden') {
  1058→                            console.log('🔧 Preventing corporate navigation from being hidden');
  1059→                            target.style.display = 'block';
  1060→                            target.style.visibility = 'visible';
  1061→                        }
  1062→                    }
  1063→                }
  1064→            });
  1065→        });
  1066→        
  1067→        observer.observe(navItem, { attributes: true, subtree: true });
  1068→        if (subNav) {
  1069→            observer.observe(subNav, { attributes: true, subtree: true });
  1070→        }
  1071→        
  1072→        console.log('🔧 Navigation item expanded and protected from hiding');
  1073→    }
  1074→
  1075→    function findHeadingByText(text) {
  1076→        // Helper function to find headings by text content
  1077→        const headings = document.querySelectorAll('h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6');
  1078→        for (const heading of headings) {
  1079→            if (heading.textContent.trim().toLowerCase().includes(text.toLowerCase())) {
  1080→                return heading;
  1081→            }
  1082→        }
  1083→        return null;
  1084→    }
  1085→
  1086→    function setupCorporateContentScrollSpy(navList, sections) {
  1087→        console.log('🔍 Setting up scroll spy for corporate content navigation...');
  1088→        
  1089→        let ticking = false;
  1090→        let lastActiveSection = null;
  1091→        let scrollSpyActive = false;
  1092→        
  1093→        function updateActiveNavigation() {
  1094→            if (!navList || !sections) return;
  1095→            
  1096→            // Find which section is currently visible
  1097→            let activeSection = null;
  1098→            const scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
  1099→            
  1100→            // Check each section to find the currently visible one
  1101→            for (let i = sections.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
  1102→                const section = sections[i];
  1103→                const targetElement = document.getElementById(section.id) || 
  1104→                                   document.querySelector(`h${section.level}[id="${section.id}"]`) ||
  1105→                                   findHeadingByText(section.title);
  1106→                
  1107→                if (targetElement) {
  1108→                    const rect = targetElement.getBoundingClientRect();
  1109→                    const elementTop = rect.top + scrollTop;
  1110→                    
  1111→                    // Consider element active if it's within the viewport or just passed
  1112→                    if (elementTop <= scrollTop + 100) {
  1113→                        activeSection = section;
  1114→                        break;
  1115→                    }
  1116→                }
  1117→            }
  1118→            
  1119→            // Update navigation highlighting if section changed
  1120→            if (activeSection && activeSection.id !== lastActiveSection) {
  1121→                // ONLY remove active state from corporate sub-navigation links, not main nav
  1122→                navList.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link').forEach(link => {
  1123→                    link.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active');
  1124→                });
  1125→                
  1126→                // Add active state to current section's nav link
  1127→                const activeLink = navList.querySelector(`a[href="#${activeSection.id}"]`);
  1128→                if (activeLink) {
  1129→                    activeLink.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
  1130→                    console.log(`🔍 Corporate active section: ${activeSection.title}`);
  1131→                }
  1132→                
  1133→                lastActiveSection = activeSection.id;
  1134→            }
  1135→            
  1136→            ticking = false;
  1137→        }
  1138→        
  1139→        function onScroll() {
  1140→            if (!ticking) {
  1141→                requestAnimationFrame(updateActiveNavigation);
  1142→                ticking = true;
  1143→            }
  1144→        }
  1145→

     1→/**
     2→ * Corporate Content Loader
     3→ * 
     4→ * Handles loading and decrypting corporate content when accessed from 
     5→ * BMW corporate network. Works with content encrypted by encrypt-corporate-content.js
     6→ */
     7→
     8→(function() {
     9→    'use strict';
    10→
    11→    // Corporate content loader class
    12→    // Cache buster: 2025-09-21T14:12:00Z - Fixed coder-workspaces.png 404 error
    13→    class CorporateContentLoader {
    14→        constructor() {
    15→            // Use assets directory path to bypass GitHub Pages filtering
    16→            this.encryptedContentPath = '/agentic-ai-nano/assets/data/corporate-content.js';
    17→            console.log('🔍 Corporate content path configured:', this.encryptedContentPath);
    18→            console.log('🔍 Current pathname:', window.location.pathname);
    19→            console.log('🔍 Current hostname:', window.location.hostname);
    20→            this.corporateKey = 'bmw-corporate-network-2024-secure'; // Same as encryption script
    21→            this.loadedContent = null;
    22→            this._isReplacingContent = false; // Flag to prevent duplicate content replacement
    23→        }
    24→
    25→        /**
    26→         * Derives the same key used for encryption
    27→         */
    28→        async deriveKey(passphrase) {
    29→            const encoder = new TextEncoder();
    30→            const data = encoder.encode(passphrase);
    31→            const hashBuffer = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', data);
    32→            return await crypto.subtle.importKey(
    33→                'raw',
    34→                hashBuffer,
    35→                { name: 'AES-GCM' },
    36→                false,
    37→                ['decrypt']
    38→            );
    39→        }
    40→
    41→        /**
    42→         * Decrypts content using AES-GCM
    43→         */
    44→        async decryptContent(encryptedData, key) {
    45→            try {
    46→                const iv = this.base64ToArrayBuffer(encryptedData.iv);
    47→                const authTag = this.base64ToArrayBuffer(encryptedData.authTag);
    48→                const encrypted = this.base64ToArrayBuffer(encryptedData.encrypted);
    49→                
    50→                // Combine encrypted data with auth tag for AES-GCM
    51→                const ciphertext = new Uint8Array(encrypted.byteLength + authTag.byteLength);
    52→                ciphertext.set(new Uint8Array(encrypted), 0);
    53→                ciphertext.set(new Uint8Array(authTag), encrypted.byteLength);
    54→
    55→                const decrypted = await crypto.subtle.decrypt(
    56→                    {
    57→                        name: 'AES-GCM',
    58→                        iv: iv,
    59→                        tagLength: 128
    60→                    },
    61→                    key,
    62→                    ciphertext
    63→                );
    64→
    65→                return new TextDecoder().decode(decrypted);
    66→            } catch (error) {
    67→                console.error('Decryption failed:', error);
    68→                throw new Error('Failed to decrypt corporate content');
    69→            }
    70→        }
    71→
    72→        /**
    73→         * Converts base64 string to ArrayBuffer
    74→         */
    75→        base64ToArrayBuffer(base64) {
    76→            const binaryString = atob(base64);
    77→            const bytes = new Uint8Array(binaryString.length);
    78→            for (let i = 0; i < binaryString.length; i++) {
    79→                bytes[i] = binaryString.charCodeAt(i);
    80→            }
    81→            return bytes.buffer;
    82→        }
    83→
    84→        /**
    85→         * Checks if corporate content is needed for the current page
    86→         */
    87→        isCorporateContentNeeded() {
    88→            const currentPath = window.location.pathname;
    89→            const needsCorporateContent = 
    90→                currentPath.includes('/00_intro/coder/') ||
    91→                currentPath.includes('/00_intro/llmapi/') ||
    92→                currentPath.includes('/03_mcp-acp-a2a/Session10_Enterprise_Integration_Production_Deployment/');
    93→            
    94→            console.log(`🔍 Corporate content needed for ${currentPath}: ${needsCorporateContent}`);
    95→            return needsCorporateContent;
    96→        }
    97→
    98→        /**
    99→         * Loads and decrypts corporate content from inline HTML comments
   100→         */

    26→// Function to inject content into HTML file
    27→function injectContentIntoHtml(filePath) {
    28→    try {

    30→

    34→            return;
    35→        }

    39→<!-- ENCRYPTED_CORPORATE_CONTENT_START
    40→${encryptedContent}
    41→ENCRYPTED_CORPORATE_CONTENT_END -->`;
    42→        
    43→        // Inject before closing body tag
    44→        if (htmlContent.includes('</body>')) {
    45→            htmlContent = htmlContent.replace('</body>', `${injectionComment}\n</body>`);
    46→            fs.writeFileSync(filePath, htmlContent, 'utf8');
    47→            console.log('✅ Injected into:', path.relative(SITE_DIR, filePath));
    48→        } else {
    49→            console.log('⚠️  No </body> tag found in:', path.relative(SITE_DIR, filePath));
    50→        }

     1→# 🏭 Session 10: Enterprise Integration & Production Deployment in BMW Cloud Environment
     2→
     3→## From Innovation Labs to Production Reality: Deploying AI Agents in Corporate Infrastructure
     4→
     5→Picture this: You've built an elegant multi-agent system that can solve complex problems, coordinate workflows, and deliver intelligent insights. It works beautifully in your development environment, demos flawlessly to stakeholders, and passes every technical review. But now comes the ultimate challenge—deploying this digital intelligence into the real world of enterprise infrastructure, where security policies are non-negotiable, compliance is legally mandated, and downtime isn't just inconvenient—it's business-critical.
     6→
     7→Welcome to BMW's cloud environment, where automotive engineering meets cutting-edge AI infrastructure. Here, we don't just deploy agents; we integrate them into a sophisticated ecosystem that must meet the rigorous standards of one of the world's leading automotive manufacturers. Every connection is secured, every API call is monitored, every resource allocation is optimized, and every deployment must align with both technical excellence and regulatory compliance.
     8→
     9→This isn't just about Kubernetes and containers—it's about creating a production-grade AI platform that can scale from prototype to enterprise deployment while maintaining the security, reliability, and performance standards that BMW's business operations demand.
    10→
    11→*Welcome to Enterprise Integration & Production Deployment—where innovation meets industrial-grade infrastructure.*
    12→
    13→![BMW Cloud Room Architecture](images/bmw-cloud-room-architecture.png)
    14→
    15→## 🎯📝⚙️ Learning Path Overview
    16→
    17→This session offers three distinct learning paths designed to match your enterprise deployment goals:
    18→
    19→=== "🎯 Observer (60-90 min)"
    20→
    21→    **Focus**: Understanding enterprise deployment architecture and BMW cloud infrastructure
    22→    
    23→    **Activities**: Cloud room concepts, Coder platform overview, security considerations
    24→    
    25→    **Ideal for**: Decision makers, architects, enterprise stakeholders
    26→
    27→=== "📝 Participant (4-6 hours)"
    28→
    29→    **Focus**: Hands-on deployment using BMW's Coder environment
    30→    
    31→    **Activities**: Workspace creation, MCP/A2A deployment, monitoring setup
    32→    
    33→    **Ideal for**: Developers, technical leads, platform engineers
    34→
    35→=== "⚙️ Implementer (12-16 hours)"
    36→
    37→    **Focus**: Complete enterprise-scale deployment with advanced configurations
    38→    
    39→    **Activities**: Custom templates, advanced security, monitoring, cost optimization
    40→    
    41→    **Ideal for**: Senior engineers, platform architects, DevOps specialists
    42→
    43→## 🎯 Observer Path: BMW Cloud Infrastructure Overview
    44→
    45→### The BMW Cloud Environment: Where Engineering Meets Innovation
    46→
    47→BMW's approach to cloud development reflects the same precision and attention to detail that goes into manufacturing world-class vehicles. Just as every component in a BMW is carefully engineered, tested, and integrated into a cohesive system, our cloud infrastructure follows the same principles of excellence.
    48→
    49→### Core Infrastructure: The Foundation
    50→

    15→Atomic Agents represent the next evolution in agent architecture, embracing the principle that complex systems should be built from simple, composable, and reusable components. Like LEGO blocks, each atomic agent is designed to be self-contained yet seamlessly interoperable with others.
    16→
    17→This session introduces a paradigm shift from monolithic agent frameworks to atomic, modular architectures that scale from simple tasks to enterprise systems. We'll build agents that are predictable, testable, and maintainable.
    18→
    19→![Atomic Agents Architecture](../../images/atomic-agents.png)
    20→
    21→The atomic approach transforms traditional agent development by emphasizing:  
    22→- **Single Responsibility**: Each agent handles one concern perfectly  
    23→- **Type Safety**: Schemas and validation ensure reliable data flow
